	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">List of International Cricket Council members</h1>
	
	<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
		<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
		<div id="contentSub"></div>
		
		
		
		<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>
		<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><p class="mw-empty-elt">

</p>
<div role="navigation" aria-label="Portals" class="noprint portal plainlist tright" style="margin:0.5em 0 0.5em 1em;border:solid #aaa 1px">
<ul style="display:table;box-sizing:border-box;padding:0.1em;max-width:175px;background:#f9f9f9;font-size:85%;line-height:110%;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold">
<li style="display:table-row"><span style="display:table-cell;padding:0.2em;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Cricketball.png/28px-Cricketball.png" decoding="async" width="28" height="28" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Cricketball.png/42px-Cricketball.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Cricketball.png/56px-Cricketball.png 2x" data-file-width="325" data-file-height="325" /></span><span style="display:table-cell;padding:0.2em 0.2em 0.2em 0.3em;vertical-align:middle"><a href="/wiki/Portal:Cricket" title="Portal:Cricket">Cricket portal</a></span></li></ul></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:332px;"><a href="/wiki/File:International_Cricket_Council_members_(by_status)_2017.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d1/International_Cricket_Council_members_%28by_status%29_2017.svg/330px-International_Cricket_Council_members_%28by_status%29_2017.svg.png" decoding="async" width="330" height="168" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d1/International_Cricket_Council_members_%28by_status%29_2017.svg/495px-International_Cricket_Council_members_%28by_status%29_2017.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d1/International_Cricket_Council_members_%28by_status%29_2017.svg/660px-International_Cricket_Council_members_%28by_status%29_2017.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="2754" data-file-height="1398" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:International_Cricket_Council_members_(by_status)_2017.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Current ICC Members by Membership status:<br /> <span style="background-color:#ff0000; color:black; border:1px solid darkgray; text-align:center;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</span> Full Members<br /> <span style="background-color:#ff6600; color:black; border:1px solid darkgray; text-align:center;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</span> Associate Members with <a href="/wiki/One-Day_International" class="mw-redirect" title="One-Day International">ODI</a> status<br /> <span style="background-color:#ff9900; color:black; border:1px solid darkgray; text-align:center;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</span> Associate Members<br /> <span style="background-color:#333333; color:white; border:1px solid darkgray; text-align:center;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</span> Former or suspended Members<br /> <span style="background-color:#cccccc; color:black; border:1px solid darkgray; text-align:center;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</span> Non-Members<br /></div></div></div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/International_Cricket_Council" title="International Cricket Council">International Cricket Council</a> (ICC) was founded at <a href="/wiki/Lord%27s" title="Lord&#39;s">Lord's</a> on 15 June 1909 as the Imperial Cricket Conference,<sup id="cite_ref-Role_of_the_ICC_-_International_Cricket_Council_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Role_of_the_ICC_-_International_Cricket_Council-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> with <a href="/wiki/Australian_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Australian cricket team">Australia</a>, <a href="/wiki/England_cricket_team" title="England cricket team">England</a>, and <a href="/wiki/South_African_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="South African cricket team">South Africa</a> as its founding members. In the beginning, only countries within the <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_Nations" title="Commonwealth of Nations">Commonwealth</a> could join.<sup id="cite_ref-A_Brief_History..._2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-A_Brief_History...-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> These members were then joined by <a href="/wiki/Indian_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Indian cricket team">India</a>, <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="New Zealand cricket team">New Zealand</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/West_Indies_cricket_team" title="West Indies cricket team">West Indies</a> in 1926 and later by <a href="/wiki/Pakistan_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Pakistan cricket team">Pakistan</a> in 1953.<sup id="cite_ref-International_Cricket_Council_(ICC)_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-International_Cricket_Council_(ICC)-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> In 1961, <a href="/wiki/South_African_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="South African cricket team">South Africa</a> resigned due to their leaving the Commonwealth,<sup id="cite_ref-A_Brief_History..._2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-A_Brief_History...-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> but they continued to play Test cricket until their international exile in 1970.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The Imperial Cricket Conference was renamed the International Cricket Conference in 1965, with new rules permitting countries from outside the Commonwealth to be elected into the governing body for the first time. That year, <a href="/wiki/Fiji_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Fiji cricket team">Fiji</a> and the <a href="/wiki/United_States_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="United States cricket team">USA</a> became the first Associate Member nations.<sup id="cite_ref-A_Brief_History..._2-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-A_Brief_History...-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In 1981, <a href="/wiki/Sri_Lankan_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Sri Lankan cricket team">Sri Lanka</a> became the first Associate Member to be elected a Full Member, returning the number of Test-playing nations to seven. In 1989, the ICC was again renamed, this time to International Cricket Council.<sup id="cite_ref-A_Brief_History..._2-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-A_Brief_History...-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> South Africa was reelected as a Full Member to the ICC in 1991 and <a href="/wiki/Zimbabwe_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Zimbabwe cricket team">Zimbabwe</a> was elected in 1992.<sup id="cite_ref-International_Cricket_Council_(ICC)_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-International_Cricket_Council_(ICC)-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> It would be eight years before the next Full Member, <a href="/wiki/Bangladesh_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Bangladesh cricket team">Bangladesh</a>, was elected in 2000.<sup id="cite_ref-International_Cricket_Council_(ICC)_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-International_Cricket_Council_(ICC)-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> On 22 June 2017, <a href="/wiki/Ireland_cricket_team" title="Ireland cricket team">Ireland</a> and <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan_national_cricket_team" title="Afghanistan national cricket team">Afghanistan</a> were granted Full Member and Test status, bringing the number of Full Members to 12.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As of 29 July 2019, there are 104 ICC members, with 12 Full Members and 92 Associate Members. The Membership Committee will consider all future requests for membership – full and associate – against an objective set of criteria. There was previously a third level, Affiliate Membership, which was removed in June 2017 with all previous Affiliate Members becoming Associate Members.<sup id="cite_ref-Assoc_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Assoc-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> The rule changes introduced a <a href="/wiki/Hierarchy" title="Hierarchy">hierarchy</a>, with two categories of membership: Full Members and Associate Members. Any new member elected to the governing body could only be an Associate Member, with the possibility of later being promoted to a Full Member based on ongoing performance in international competition.
</p><p>In July 2019, the ICC suspended <a href="/wiki/Zimbabwe_Cricket" title="Zimbabwe Cricket">Zimbabwe Cricket</a>, the first time this has been done to a Full Member side.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div id="toc" class="toc"><input type="checkbox" role="button" id="toctogglecheckbox" class="toctogglecheckbox" style="display:none" /><div class="toctitle" lang="en" dir="ltr"><h2>Contents</h2><span class="toctogglespan"><label class="toctogglelabel" for="toctogglecheckbox"></label></span></div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Full_Members">Full Members</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_International_Cricket_Council_members&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Full Members">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Full Members are the governing bodies for cricket in a country or a group of associated countries representing a geographical area. All Full Members have a right to send one representative team to play official Test matches and have full voting rights at meetings of the ICC. Also, all Full Member nations are automatically qualified to play <a href="/wiki/One-Day_International" class="mw-redirect" title="One-Day International">ODIs</a> and <a href="/wiki/T20I" class="mw-redirect" title="T20I">T20Is</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-A_Brief_History..._2-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-A_Brief_History...-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> The West Indies cricket team does not represent one country, but rather an amalgamation of more than 15 countries and territories from the <a href="/wiki/Caribbean" title="Caribbean">Caribbean</a>. The English Cricket team represents both <a href="/wiki/England_and_Wales" title="England and Wales">England and Wales</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Ireland_cricket_team" title="Ireland cricket team">Ireland cricket team</a> represents <a href="/wiki/All-Ireland" title="All-Ireland">all of the island of Ireland</a>.
</p><p>Among these 12 nations, <a href="/wiki/Sri_Lanka_national_cricket_team" title="Sri Lanka national cricket team">Sri Lanka</a>, <a href="/wiki/Zimbabwe_national_cricket_team" title="Zimbabwe national cricket team">Zimbabwe</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bangladesh_national_cricket_team" title="Bangladesh national cricket team">Bangladesh</a>, <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan_national_cricket_team" title="Afghanistan national cricket team">Afghanistan</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ireland_cricket_team" title="Ireland cricket team">Ireland</a> have played as associate nations under the ICC before becoming Full Members. Currently, Zimbabwe is suspended by the ICC.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Associate_Members">Associate Members</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_International_Cricket_Council_members&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Associate Members">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Associate Members are countries where cricket is firmly established and organised but do not qualify for Full Membership.<sup id="cite_ref-A_Brief_History..._2-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-A_Brief_History...-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> There are 92 Associate Members.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>All Associates are eligible to play in the <a href="/wiki/ICC_World_Cricket_League" class="mw-redirect" title="ICC World Cricket League">ICC World Cricket League</a>, a series of international one-day cricket administered by the ICC.<sup id="cite_ref-World_Cricket_League_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-World_Cricket_League-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> There is also an <a href="/wiki/ICC_T20_World_Cup_Qualifier" title="ICC T20 World Cup Qualifier">ICC T20 World Cup Qualifier</a> that works as a qualification process for <a href="/wiki/ICC_T20_World_Cup" title="ICC T20 World Cup">ICC T20 World Cup</a> that occurred every two years (until 2016, the next T20 World Cup is in 2020). Until April 2018, only  the qualified teams were awarded <a href="/wiki/Twenty20_International" title="Twenty20 International">Twenty20 International status</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> In April 2018, the ICC announced T20I status for all its members from 1 July 2018 for women's game and from 1 January 2019 for men's game.<sup id="cite_ref-ICC2019_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ICC2019-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In addition to key administrative requirements of the national governing body, an Associate Member must:<sup id="cite_ref-accociate_criteria_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-accociate_criteria-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>have a minimum of 16 senior teams and 16 junior teams playing in a structured competition or competitions;</li>
<li>have access to at least 8 cricket grounds, 4 of which must have a permanent pitch.</li></ul>
<p><i><img alt="dagger" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/37/Dagger-14-plain.png" decoding="async" width="9" height="14" data-file-width="9" data-file-height="14" />Denotes members that are currently suspended by the ICC.</i>
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Associate_Members_with_ODI_status">Associate Members with ODI status</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_International_Cricket_Council_members&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Associate Members with ODI status">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/International_Cricket_Council" title="International Cricket Council">ICC</a> grants <a href="/wiki/One-Day_International" class="mw-redirect" title="One-Day International">One-Day International</a> status to its Associate Members based on their success in the <a href="/wiki/World_Cricket_League" title="World Cricket League">World Cricket League</a>.
</p><p>The Associate teams who currently hold <a href="/wiki/One-Day_International" class="mw-redirect" title="One-Day International">ODI</a> status are:
</p>
<table class="wikitable sortable">

<tbody><tr>
<th>Team
</th>
<th>Governing body
</th>
<th>ODI status since
</th>
<th>Region
</th>
<th>Current <a href="/wiki/ICC_ODI_Championship" title="ICC ODI Championship">ODI</a> Ranking
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Flag_of_Namibia.svg/23px-Flag_of_Namibia.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Flag_of_Namibia.svg/35px-Flag_of_Namibia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Flag_of_Namibia.svg/45px-Flag_of_Namibia.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Namibia_national_cricket_team" title="Namibia national cricket team">Namibia</a>
</td>

</td>
<td><span data-sort-value="000000002019-01-01-0000" style="white-space:nowrap">2019</span><sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup>

</tbody></table>
<p>In winning the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9317_ICC_World_Cricket_League_Championship" title="2015–17 ICC World Cricket League Championship">2015–17 World Cricket League</a>, <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_national_cricket_team" title="Netherlands national cricket team">Netherlands</a> ensured they would become an ODI team at the end of the <a href="/wiki/2018_Cricket_World_Cup_Qualifier" title="2018 Cricket World Cup Qualifier">2018 World Cup Qualifier</a>. The three other highest placed associates in this qualifier (UAE, Scotland and Nepal) joined them. In June 2018, Scotland and UAE were added to the main ODI rankings list, with Nepal joining them in January 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup>  Netherlands will be added once they have played enough games to gain a meaningful rating.
</p><p>Four additional teams gained ODI status after the conclusion of the <a href="/wiki/2019_ICC_World_Cricket_League_Division_Two" title="2019 ICC World Cricket League Division Two">World Cricket League Division Two</a> tournament in April 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-ICC_103-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ICC-103">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> These teams were <a href="/wiki/Namibia_national_cricket_team" title="Namibia national cricket team">Namibia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Oman_national_cricket_team" title="Oman national cricket team">Oman</a>, <a href="/wiki/Papua_New_Guinea_national_cricket_team" title="Papua New Guinea national cricket team">Papua New Guinea</a> and <a href="/wiki/United_States_national_cricket_team" title="United States national cricket team">USA</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-ICC_103-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ICC-103">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Associate_Members_with_T20I_status">Associate Members with T20I status</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_International_Cricket_Council_members&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Associate Members with T20I status">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In April 2018, the ICC announced T20I status for all its 105 Members from 1 January 2019. Therefore, all <a href="/wiki/Twenty20" title="Twenty20">Twenty20</a> matches played between ICC Members after 1 January 2019 will be full T20I.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ICC2019_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ICC2019-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Former_members">Former members</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_International_Cricket_Council_members&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Former members">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>There are five countries who were previously members of the International Cricket Council (associate or affiliate), but had their memberships revoked due to various reasons.

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Regional_bodies">Regional bodies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_International_Cricket_Council_members&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Regional bodies">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Regional bodies aim to organise, promote and develop the game of cricket in their respective ICC regions:
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/African_Cricket_Association" title="African Cricket Association">African Cricket Association</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Asian_Cricket_Council" title="Asian Cricket Council">Asian Cricket Council</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/ICC_Americas" title="ICC Americas">ICC Americas</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/ICC_East_Asia-Pacific" title="ICC East Asia-Pacific">ICC East Asia-Pacific</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/European_Cricket_Council" title="European Cricket Council">European Cricket Council</a></li></ul>
<p>Two further regional bodies were disestablished following the creation of the African Cricket Association:
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/East_and_Central_Africa_Cricket_Council" class="mw-redirect" title="East and Central Africa Cricket Council">East and Central Africa Cricket Council</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/West_Africa_Cricket_Council" title="West Africa Cricket Council">West Africa Cricket Council</a></li></ul>
